Current Affairs Commentary

National Government Orders to Punish Zhang 48

---Middle

The Xi'an Incident occurred suddenly. The military leader, whom the entire nation looked up to, was unexpectedly kidnapped and lost his freedom. Other important military officers responsible for the suppression were also concentrated under the guise of seeking an audience and were detained by force. At a time when the diplomatic situation is unusually tense and the war on the border is in progress, such an unpredictable storm has arisen in the rear, causing the people a shock that cannot be calmed and increasing the precariousness of the situation. The strength of unity is reverting to disunity. Who caused this? No matter what excuses Zhang Xueliang makes, it will be difficult for him to explain himself to the people.

Regarding this sudden incident, the central government, in addition to grief and indignation, still puts national affairs first and does not want to resort to arms lightly. Therefore, on the one hand, it only maintains the authority of the central government by stripping Zhang of his position and investigating him. On the other hand, it hopes that Chiang Kai-shek will be sent back to Nanjing, hinting at Zhang's self-renewal. In recent days, letters and telegrams from various parties advising Zhang have been widely published in newspapers, but the serious impact of the Shaanxi Incident has not shown any signs of turning around. This means that Zhang Xueliang has no intention of repentance and is determined to disrupt the overall situation. Even if the government has the pain of compromising and seeking perfection, it is difficult to sit idly by and ignore the rebellion. Therefore, yesterday, with the approval of the Central Political Council, the National Government issued an order to punish the rebels, and He Yingqin was appointed as the Commander-in-Chief of the punitive expedition. It is expected that in the event of a punitive expedition, it will be difficult to distinguish between the innocent and the guilty. The government takes rectifying discipline as a prerequisite, and it has no choice but to do so. However, Zhang, by creating the fact with his own hands, has caused innocent lives to suffer the same fate, destroyed the situation of unity, destroyed the strength against foreign forces, and turned years of hard work into nothing. The unanimous expectation of the whole country has been reversed. How great is our heartache and disappointment?

In short, now that things have come to this, we no longer want to discuss the merits and demerits. We can only remain calm and united, support the government's policy, and take firm steps. If Zhang's subordinates have a desire to repent, they should repent as soon as possible, so that the punitive expedition can be quickly concluded and the entire strength will not be destroyed. We must not let those close to us grieve and those who hate us rejoice. This is what we earnestly pray for.

The League of Nations' Technical Cooperation Program for China Next Year: Experts to be Sent to China for Consultation, League of Nations Committee has Approved. 49

(Geneva) The League of Nations Committee on Technical Cooperation with China met this morning to discuss the cooperation program for 1937. My representative, Guo Taiqi, said that the Chinese government was very satisfied with the League of Nations' dispatch of experts to China and requested that more assistance be provided by experts in specific and detailed plans for water conservancy and highway projects in the future. League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol replied that he would do his best to assist and suggested establishing a planning office in Nanjing, headed by three engineering experts. The Chinese government also plans to invite Strickland to be a senior rural technical advisor and to add a public administration expert. Strickland has expressed his willingness to take the position of advisor, but an administrative expert has not yet been selected. Regarding the dispatch of Chinese experts to Europe, the Chinese government and the League of Nations have formulated several rules for implementation. However, due to the tight budget next year, only half of the planned number of experts can be sent to Europe. Avenol also intends to tighten up the budget so that more people can be sent. Although the budget for next year is not generous, it is planned to be distributed and used carefully to avoid waste. (Central News Agency dispatch, 15th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Committee on Technical Cooperation with China held a meeting here this morning. In addition to the Chinese representative, Ambassador to the United Kingdom Guo Taiqi, representatives from the United Kingdom, France, Chile, Romania, Sweden, and other countries attended. The US government also sent observers to the meeting, which was chaired by Chilean representative Ordine. The committee passed the 1937 technical cooperation budget and program submitted by the League of Nations Secretariat. The program stipulates that in the near future, the League of Nations will send experts and civil servants to China, and provide the Chinese government with convenience for sending personnel abroad for inspection. The work plan is roughly divided into the following items: (1) Regarding agriculture, it stipulates various measures for developing agricultural cooperatives in China; (2) Regarding transportation, the League of Nations plans to appoint three engineers to provide consultation to Chinese competent technical agencies on highway construction issues and to train senior Chinese engineering personnel; (3) Regarding administrative organization, it plans to send an expert in public administration affairs to provide consultation to the Chinese government; (4) Regarding Chinese experts going abroad for inspection, it is stipulated that the Chinese government will send several public health experts, one engineer, one senior official from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, one expert on rural revitalization issues, and one financial expert to go abroad for inspection. After discussion by the Technical Cooperation Committee, the program and budget案 were immediately approved. Finally, Chinese representative Guo Taiqi spoke, expressing his thanks and saying that this technical cooperation method would be greatly beneficial to both the League of Nations and China. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

Representatives of American Countries Sign Draft of Neutrality Convention, Containing Seven Articles, Still to be Submitted to the General Assembly for Approval 50

Argentine Capital. Representatives of the twenty-one countries at the American Peace Conference have signed the final draft of the Neutrality Convention today, preparing to submit it to the plenary session for approval on Friday and Saturday of this week. Although Argentina has signed the treaty, it reserves the right to grant loans and supply food to belligerent countries in wartime. Colombia also has reservations about the definition of the word "aggressor." The draft treaty contains the following points:

(1) Reaffirming the obligations of various existing treaties in the Americas.

(2) American countries must consult with each other when peace is in danger.

(3) If the signatory countries believe that there is a danger of war, they must invoke items (1) and (2).

(4) Any disputes must be resolved in accordance with existing treaties.

(5) If there is a war, the signatory countries must also be bound by existing treaties.

(6) Reaffirming the policy of neutrality in wartime and banning the export of arms.

(7) This convention does not affect the rights and obligations of League of Nations member states.

(8) This convention is indefinite, but signatory countries may withdraw by notifying one year in advance. (National dispatch, 15th)

Deferred for Discussion at Next General Assembly

Argentine Capital. Ribbentrop Speech: Germany Needs Colonies, Says Communism Gains Ground, World Peace Difficult to Achieve 55

(London) German Ambassador to the United Kingdom General Ribbentrop, in his first public speech to a British audience at the Grosvenor House tonight, solemnly stated that the resolution of the colonial issue has long been a matter of concern. German leader Hitler is deeply aware that Germany should have colonies to supply the raw materials needed by its country and to restore its world trade, which are two essential measures to improve the current standard of living of the German people. If conflict recurs between Britain and Germany, or creates a world war, it will inevitably lead to a great victory for Bolshevism. Ribbentrop expressed regret that Hitler's repeated proposals to reduce armaments and conclude non-aggression pacts and other peace treaties have all failed. He continued that he believed that if destructive communism continues to gain ground, the world will ultimately be unable to restore order and have peaceful development. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

Germany has decided to get rid of all discriminatory clauses in the Treaty of Versailles, but our leader Hitler is still willing to establish agreements with all countries in the world in order to achieve the goal. Unfortunately, all countries have turned a deaf ear." Former Aviation Minister Lord Londonderry then took the floor and advocated that German leader Hitler, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, French Prime Minister Blum, and British Prime Minister Baldwin should hold a conference and announce to the world that "war will never happen." British New Emperor Relies on Old Ministers of the Previous Dynasty 62

Wigram Appointed as Advisor

(London) British New Emperor George VI announced his first appointment today, which has aroused special attention among the general public, because it is known from the people he has appointed that the Emperor has a tendency to rely on old ministers of the previous dynasty. For example, Lord Wigram, who recently retired, has been serving in the palace since 1910 and is one of the old ministers of the previous dynasty, has now been appointed as Permanent Lord-in-Waiting and Advisor, which is one example. Wigram served as Secretary to George V and Edward VIII until he resigned in July of this year. Harding, who succeeded Wigram as Secretary to Edward VIII, will continue to serve as Private Secretary to the New Emperor George VI, but due to overwork in this constitutional crisis, he has been granted three months of leave to recuperate. Harding served as Assistant Secretary and Extra Equerry to George V for sixteen years. (Reuters dispatch, 16th)

Dispute Between Turkey and France, League of Nations Council Passes Resolution on Transitional Measures, Sends Personnel to Syria for Inspection, Turkish Representative Unilaterally Abstains from Voting 64

(Geneva) The League of Nations Council held a meeting this morning and immediately discussed the issue of the Turkish minority in Alexandretta and Antioch in Syria, and unanimously passed a resolution on transitional measures (i.e., various measures to be taken before the League of Nations Council thoroughly discusses the issue in January next year). However, Turkish representative Rüştü abstained from voting. At the beginning of the meeting today, the reporter, Swedish Foreign Minister Sandler, read out the draft resolution, the content of which was proposed by the French government, and there were three points: (1) Send three inspectors to inspect and report to the League of Nations Council. Once the Council meets in January next year, the task of each inspector will be completed; (2) The French government once sent reinforcements to Antioch to quell the disturbances that occurred earlier and is willing to withdraw them, but the normal number of troops stationed will be maintained; (3) France promises not to submit the treaty signed between France and Syria (i.e., the treaty allowing Syria's independence) to Congress for approval before the meeting in January next year. French representative Weygand then rose and spoke in the name of the French government, saying that the transitional measures proposed by Turkish representative Rüştü, namely sending a neutral police force and establishing an international provisional co-management system, could not be accepted, because these measures endanger the privileges enjoyed by the mandatory power under the current system in Alexandretta and Antioch. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

(Geneva) Regarding the issue of the Turkish minority in Alexandretta and Antioch in Syria, the Council of the League of Nations did not have time to hold a meeting this afternoon and postponed it to tomorrow. The reporter on this issue, Swedish Foreign Minister Sandler, had a long conversation with French representative Weygand and Turkish representative Rüştü this afternoon, and they had generally agreed on transitional measures to resolve the issue. The French and Turkish representatives have both agreed to send neutral observers to the cities. The French representative also promised to withdraw the troops sent by France to Antioch when disturbances occurred earlier in the two cities, but the normal number of French troops stationed would still be maintained. In addition, France also allows not to submit the treaty signed between France and Syria (i.e., the treaty allowing Syria's independence) to Congress for approval before the League of Nations Council thoroughly discusses this issue in January next year. However, the French position has a basic point, that is, if the Council of the League of Nations makes any decision at present, it must be limited to strict transitional measures, and these transitional measures must not damage the rights of the mandatory power, because these rights are stipulated in the permanent ruling system of the two cities. Tonight at 10 o'clock, Sandler will continue to hold talks with Weygand and Rüştü to determine several details on which the two sides have not yet agreed. For example, whether Turkish observers can be added to the observers sent to the two cities, in addition to neutral people, must also be determined. It is generally hoped that when the Council holds a meeting at 11:30 tomorrow morning, the French and Turkish sides will be able to reach a complete compromise. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

French Senate Discusses Mandatory Arbitration Bill 66

(Paris) The Senate discussed the mandatory arbitration bill for labor disputes today, and former Minister of Justice Senator Le Mer proposed to postpone the discussion of the bill, saying that the government had previously allowed Senator Bianvenou of the left-wing Radical Democratic Party to find a way to prevent workers from occupying factories, but the facts of destroying property rights are still continuing, so the case should be postponed for discussion. The chairman of the Senate Commerce Committee, Duruy, immediately expressed his opposition and said that the national economy is currently in a crisis of collapse, and the Senate has no right to delay the vote on this bill to mediate labor disputes. At this point, Senator Foulquier questioned whether the government has the sincerity to implement various orders regarding preventing the occupation of factories and resolutely try to prevent such incidents. Prime Minister Blum replied that there were a total of 147 incidents of workers occupying factories, of which 115 have been resolved, and the workers have withdrawn from the factories. In addition, 32 cases are in the process of being resolved quickly. Currently, there are no more than 2,400 striking workers in the Paris area. Workers occupying factories in Lille have all withdrawn, and the factories in Mulhouse will soon follow suit. If it is said that labor disputes still exist, then I should ask you to quickly pass the mandatory arbitration bill so that these disputes can be resolved quickly, amicably, and legally. At this point, the Senate rejected Le Mer's motion to postpone the discussion with a majority of 207 votes to 59. Subsequently, the Senate announced the end of the debate and decided to hold another meeting at 10:00 on Thursday morning to discuss the articles of the bill one by one. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

British Chancellor Announces Increase in Bank Reserves of £65 Million 68

(London) Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain announced in the House of Commons today that the British government has decided to increase the reserves of the Bank of England's note issuing department by £65 million as an expedient measure. This step is tantamount to a sudden expansion of the credit base, which is not currently necessary. Therefore, at the request of the bank, I have exercised the power conferred on the government by the Currency and Bank Notes Act of 1928, ordering a reduction of £60 million in the fiduciary note issue, so that the expansion is limited to a small extent. This measure has no greater cause than being timely and appropriate. The fiduciary issue can be increased or decreased at any time in accordance with the aforementioned act. Business circles are quite puzzled by the Bank of England's purchase of £65 million in cash from the Exchange Equalisation Account while simultaneously reducing the fiduciary note issue by £60 million, leading to divided opinions. However, most people believe that this move can indicate the government's confidence in resisting the pressure on the pound caused by the possible repatriation of funds from France and the potential outflow of cash to Wall Street, using the large amount of cash held in the Exchange Equalisation Account. It is also said that when the pound has a strong upward trend, it is best to restore the free activity of the Exchange Equalisation Account, as the account can curb the depreciation of the pound by selling some of its gold reserves. (Reuters, 15th)

Lisbon. The Portuguese government submitted its reply yesterday to the British and French governments' proposal for mediating the Spanish Civil War and holding a plebiscite for the Spanish people, refusing to accept it. The reply stated that Portugal would consider any proposals that would safeguard peace in Spain, but it would not be appropriate to ignore its own interests. (Havas, 16th)

Lisbon. Portugal's reply to the British and French proposals for mediating the Spanish Civil War was released by the Portuguese authorities today. The document expressed doubt about the feasibility of mediation and declared that this was a struggle between civilization and barbarism. Unless one side gains complete victory and establishes a strong and generous government, mediation would only be a temporary truce, and a more severe war would follow. Rebel Troops Capture Important Town in Madrid Suburbs 71

Dalaara. A special dispatch from our correspondent states that the Nationalist forces captured the town of Boadilla, on the western outskirts of Madrid, yesterday. The government forces suffered heavy casualties in this battle, with as many as 200 corpses abandoned in the Duke of Tésuega's mansion alone. The Duke's mansion was filled with ammunition, like an arsenal, with 22 machine guns already aimed and 38 more in reserve. Captain Suber, who commanded the garrison in the headquarters, was first killed by the Nationalist forces, which greatly angered the garrison, who resisted fiercely, but were eventually defeated by the Nationalist forces. (Havas, 16th)

Madrid. The Madrid Defense Committee issued a communiqué today stating that the rebel forces continued to attack the government forces' positions in the areas of Boadilla and Terramonte. The attacking rebel forces belonged to the Foreign Legion, and after being repeatedly repelled by the government forces, they suffered heavy losses and were finally forced to retreat to their original lines. The communiqué also stated that the weather is currently severe, and after a lull in the fighting on the Burgos front, the government forces recently attacked Viéldu, destroying the rebel forces' positions. (Reuters, 16th)

Madrid. The Defense Committee issued a communiqué this morning announcing an important victory for the government forces. It was claimed that in the battle of Boadilla del Monte, southwest of Madrid, last night, after nine hours of fierce fighting, the rebel forces were completely defeated. Two hundred rebel soldiers were killed in the government forces' lines, and many more were wounded. This attack by the rebel forces was one of three attempts, but each attempt resulted in heavy casualties and retreat. It is reported that Moroccan and German troops also participated in this battle. The enemy forces charged forward under the cover of several aircraft and many tanks, but after being strafed by government forces' machine guns, they retreated in disarray. (Reuters, 16th)

Russo-Japanese Fisheries Agreement Issue; Japanese Government Decides Policy; Urge Russia to Sign Within Two Months, Otherwise Ensure Rights and Interests by Means of Goods 75

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Hirota, Foreign Minister Arita, Navy Minister Nagano, Army Minister Terauchi, Agriculture Minister Shimada, etc., stayed in the Imperial Palace after the plenary session of the Privy Council on the 16th to hold a five-minister conference to hold important discussions on the Japan-Soviet fisheries treaty. Foreign Minister Arita first stated the beliefs of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, followed by a firm opinion, stating that a serious protest should be made to Soviet Russia, urging it to reflect and demanding a swift signing. The four ministers Hirota, Nagano, Terauchi, and Shimada also stated various important opinions. As a result, the opinions were consistent as follows:

(1) Urge Soviet Russia to reflect seriously and urgently urge the completion of the signing of the treaty. (2) If the auction period is not signed by February of next year, take measures to ensure Japan's rights and interests, and conduct further diplomatic negotiations. (3) When implementing measures to ensure rights and interests, the Imperial Navy will stand on the high ground of justice, carry out the mission of defense, and express a firm determination not to tolerate any unjust behavior.

Here, a fundamental policy has been established regarding the fisheries treaty issue. (Domei News Agency, 16th)

Page 8

Baotou in Suiyuan Province is Resisting the Enemy; Japanese Special Agents Have Withdrawn; Radio Station Has Also Been Canceled; Market Prosperity is Gradually Returning to Its Former State 85

Suiyuan Correspondence. The reporter went to Baotou on the afternoon of yesterday and arrived at 4 o'clock. He immediately took a car to visit the airport and the Nanhai Zi area of the Yellow River Wharf, which is 20 miles south of the city. In the evening, he visited Tian Shumei, the city defense commander, the deputy chairman of the Sui-Mongolian Political Council and deputy leader of the Yi League, and A Wang, the commander of the Bao-Xi Railway Protection, as well as the county magistrate and director of the public security bureau, and talked briefly before returning to Suiyuan the next morning. The sights and sounds will be haphazardly recorded below.

Baotou City Appearance

Baotou is an important road north to the various leagues and banners of Inner Mongolia and west to Ningxia and Gansu, and it is also a water and land wharf where fur, grain, licorice, etc. are concentrated. It is the only major town in western Suiyuan. Commerce is prosperous, surpassing Suiyuan. The population is smaller in summer and autumn, about 70,000 people, which is 10,000 fewer than Suiyuan (because some citizens go to various villages to plant agricultural products). In spring and winter, about 90,000 people, which is 10,000 more than Suiyuan (because farmers move to the city after the autumn harvest and merchants from various places come to buy fur). This year, 7 to 8 million catties of fur were sold. The local value is 5 jiao per catty, and it can be sold for 6 jiao when transported to Tianjin. Sheepskin is in short supply. The sales volume and value are more than twice as high as in previous years. Because this winter happens to be the time of the war on the Sui border, the number of National Army troops increased by about 50,000. Each person needs a leather coat, which requires 3 sheets of leather, totaling 150,000 sheets. At the same time, pseudo-bandits and certain parties also bought a large amount of leather, resulting in an imbalance between supply and demand. The licorice produced in Ningxia and Inner Mongolia is transported to Baotou every year in a quantity of more than 3 million catties, and is wholesaled to merchants in various places. This year, fur merchants have made huge profits and are beaming with joy.

Japanese Activities

In Baotou, there are several Japanese people, including Nakagawaroji Hideo, Kaneya, Kuroki Shokou, and Oono Takiji from the branch office established by Hayama, renting a small courtyard in the Baotou Hotel, with a dozen rooms. A radio station is set up inside, reporting news to Changchun, Rehe, Tianjin, etc. every day. To the right of our aircraft factory, there are two aircraft rooms built by the Japanese, which have now been recovered by us through negotiations. However, Japanese aircraft still fly in from time to time, and there are fixed flights every Tuesday. It is said that when the Japanese were repairing the airfield, there were five or sixty Japanese people in Baotou every day. After serious negotiations with our side, the number gradually decreased. The Japanese previously sent special agents to the Wangfu of various banners in the Wuyi leagues, and also set up radio stations. Radio stations were also set up in Wuyuan and Gongmiaozhe, reporting news to the Japanese side at any time. Since Bailingmiao was recovered by our army, the Japanese special agents in various places have withdrawn one after another, and the radio stations have also been canceled invisibly. The importance of the recovery of Bailingmiao can be seen here. A Japanese steamship in the form of an airplane is parked on the bank of the Yellow River. It is said that it has been there for seven or eight months. Recently, the Japanese side sent 50 to 60 surveying personnel and wireless personnel to measure everywhere along the bank of the Yellow River, and also went to Wuyuan, Linhe, and other places to measure. After our side discovered this, we sent military police to monitor the ship, but we still could not dissuade them from their illegal work. Now, because the Yellow River is frozen, their work has to be stopped.

A Wang's Talk

A Wang was recently appointed by the Central Government as the commander of the first bandit suppression area on the Mongolian border, and Pan Shi as the commander of the second bandit suppression area. The reporter visited A Wang at the Baoxi Railway Protection Army Headquarters and was received. According to him, the Yi League is now very peaceful. The total population of the seven banners under its jurisdiction is less than 200,000 people, including 18,000 people in Hangjin Banner, plus 5,000 Han Chinese, more than 20,000 people in Jungar Banner, and more than 10,000 people in each of the other banners. The seven banners have a total of more than 3,000 security teams, including more than 1,300 people in Hangjin Banner, 1,500 people in Jungar Banner, and 200 people in Zhasak Banner. These security teams are not a problem for the security of the various banners.

Tian Shumei's Talk

The reporter visited Tian Shumei, the city defense commander, that evening. According to him, Baotou is now responsible for maintaining security by this brigade. In recent years, residents have been able to live and work in peace and contentment, and commerce has gradually prospered as a result. Therefore, merchants who were afraid of the bandits and dared not move forward have now resumed their old outlook. Baotou's defenses are solid, and there is no need to worry about security.

On the train, I saw many flocks of sheep, camels, and donkeys along the way. I asked the local people traveling with me, "I have often heard that there are many herds of horses and sheep in Inner Mongolia, but why are there donkeys everywhere now?" According to the answer, there were many bandits in Inner Mongolia in the past. Every autumn and winter, many herds of horses were plundered by bandits, and the residents suffered from it. Therefore, they changed to raising herds of donkeys. This is something that happened after the Republic of China. (12th)

Guangzhou Garrison Headquarters: Meeting Convened Regarding the Shaanxi Incident; Military and Political Leaders Jointly Telegraph Support for the Central Government; Banking Sector Also Discusses Measures to Stabilize Finance 86

Guangzhou Communication: News of the Xi'an Incident reached Guangdong on the evening of the 12th. By 12 o'clock that night, the Guangzhou Garrison Headquarters of the Military Affairs Commission, the Headquarters of the Fourth Route Army, and the Provincial Government had all received secret telegrams. Later, the Guangzhou branch of the Central News Agency produced and distributed a general press release. However, the release did not reach the newspapers until about 5 a.m. on the 13th. Apart from one or two newspapers that managed to publish it in time, those that did not were quick to issue special editions that day. As a result, the news spread widely, and people throughout the city were shocked. The following is a brief account of the situation in Guangdong Province over the past few days:

Military and Political Stance

In Guangdong Province, the most important military organization in name is the Guangzhou Garrison Headquarters of the Military Affairs Commission. Since Chairman Chiang Kai-shek went north, many important military officers had left Guangzhou with him. Initially, He Yingqin was internally designated as the Director of the Guangzhou Garrison Headquarters. However, due to pressing military affairs in the north, he was unable to come to Guangdong. Later, Army Commander Chen Cheng temporarily took over, but before long, Chen was also ordered to go north. Lin Weiwen, a staff officer of the Garrison Headquarters, recently returned to Nanjing due to important matters in the capital. After the Hankou Garrison Headquarters was established, the Guangzhou Garrison Headquarters transferred over thirty staff members to Hankou. Currently, the Guangzhou Garrison Headquarters retains the First and Second Departments, with Luo Zhuoying, the Army Commander of the 18th Army, acting as the Director, and Qian Zhuolun as the Director of the First Department, and Liu Jianqun as the Director of the Second Department. On the evening of the 12th, after the Garrison Headquarters suddenly received news that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek had been detained in Xi'an, Qian and Liu immediately visited Luo Zhuoying to discuss important military and political matters in Guangdong Province and consulted with Yu Hanmou, the Commander-in-Chief of the Fourth Route Army, to discuss countermeasures. As a result, on the one hand, Yu Hanmou was asked to telegraph his position, and on the other hand, he was instructed to maintain public order. Yu Hanmou issued a telegram on the 13th expressing his support for the Central Government. At noon on the 13th, the Guangzhou Garrison Headquarters convened a meeting of military officers at the Garrison Headquarters office on Da Ma Road. Those present included Luo Zhuoying, Yu Hanmou, Huang Musong, Xu Jingtang, Liu Jianqun, Li Jiang, Li Jiezhi, and others. The main points of the resolutions were as follows: (1) All military and political officials should telegraph their support for the Central Government; (2) Military and political officials should maintain calm and strictly guard against the activities of reactionary elements; (3) Maintain financial stability and investigate and apprehend bandits disrupting finance; (4) The General Headquarters of the Fourth Route Army and the Provincial Government should order all division and brigade commanders, security commanders of all districts, and administrative commissioners of all districts to strengthen local defense. At 8 a.m. on the same morning, the General Headquarters of the Fourth Route Army also convened a meeting of its officers. Those present included Commander-in-Chief Yu Hanmou, Chief of Staff Chen Mianwu, Adjutant-General Pan Yingkun, Chief of Military Affairs Wu Fan, Chief of Military Supply Ma Binghong, Chief of Ordnance Huang Yuan, Commander of the Military Police Li Jiang, Police Chief Li Jiezhi, and Division Commanders Zhang Ruigui and Mo Xide, totaling more than twenty people. They discussed the current situation for over two hours and resolved on a number of important matters, including maintaining public security and strengthening the defense of Guangdong Province. At 9 a.m. on the 14th, the generals of the Fourth Route Army and the 18th Army held a joint meeting. All military officers above the rank of major general participated, including Yu Hanmou, Luo Zhuoying, Xiang Hanping, and Xu Jingtang. The meeting adjourned at about 11 a.m.

Financial Dynamics

After the news of the Xi'an Incident spread, some merchants took the opportunity to manipulate finance. On the morning of the 13th, the exchange rate suddenly rose. Usually, the premium on Hong Kong dollars was around 52 (meaning that 100 Hong Kong dollars was worth 152 Guangdong dollars). On the afternoon of the 13th, it rose to 62. The prices of various public bonds all plummeted. Guangxi paper money had dropped to 60% of the value of Guangdong dollars (usually 80%). Finance Director Song Ziliang convened a meeting of leaders from the banking sector, the branch of the Central Bank, the branch of the Bank of China, the branch of the Bank of Communications, and the presidents of provincial and municipal banks at the Finance Department at 3 p.m. that afternoon. He announced that the provincial bank had ample reserves. Since August, the bank had issued 24,108,000 yuan in provincial silver notes, backed by 12,462,000 yuan worth of silver as cash reserve, and another 12,000,000 yuan in public bonds issued by the Ministry of Finance as guarantee reserve. Therefore, its credit was solid. Recently, due to the purchase of silver, an additional 16,500,000 yuan in provincial silver notes and 400,000 yuan in provincial silver dollars have been issued, all backed by 100% central legal tender and raw silver and gold as reserves. This shows that its financial strength is substantial. As a director of the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, he will guide the branches of these banks to assist the provincial bank. Therefore, the financial situation is as stable as a rock. Because the end of the year is approaching, the provincial bank will provide loans for the New Year to allow businesses and industries to borrow funds and facilitate turnover. By the 14th, the exchange rate had slightly decreased, with Hong Kong dollars falling to 56. However, trading remained suspended. On the afternoon of the 14th, the banking sector reconvened a meeting to discuss measures to stabilize finance. The meeting was convened by the Guangzhou Banking Association. Representatives from banks such as the Guohua Bank, the East Asia Bank, the Guangdong Bank, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Shanghai Bank, the Guohuo Bank, the Jincheng Bank, the Yanyeh Bank, and the Silk Industry Bank attended. As a result, they unanimously agreed to assist in stabilizing Guangdong silver notes and determining the ratio between the national currency and silver notes. The buying price should not exceed 5, and the selling price should not exceed 51, to stabilize finance and prices in the province. Also, on the 14th, the authorities sent personnel to secretly investigate financial manipulation. Therefore, the buying and selling of Hong Kong dollars and silver remained suspended on the 14th. As for market prices, there were no major changes, only the price of copper coins was slightly higher. Usually, 20 copper coins could be exchanged for 1 jiao, but recently only 18 could be exchanged.

Peaceful Public Security

In recent days, many rumors have circulated in the city. To maintain social order, the authorities have ordered Li Jiang, the Commander of the Military Police District, and Li Jiezhi, the Chief of Police, to dispatch military police and police to patrol day and night. After 12 o'clock at night, suspicious pedestrians are questioned. The police also pay attention to the movement of household registrations in the city and send detectives to hotels, inns, and restaurants to investigate. They also review the population of boat households to prevent criminals from hiding. The military police department has dispatched military police bicycle patrol teams, with five people in each team, totaling more than 120 teams, distributed throughout the urban area, taking turns patrolling. Outside the city, there are security teams to assist in defense. As for the Yuehan Railway, all armies under the jurisdiction of the Yue Railway Garrison Headquarters are stationed at strategic locations. Therefore, public security in the provincial capital is currently peaceful, and market trade is as usual. (December 15)

After the Occurrence of the Shaanxi Incident: Xiamen Remains Peaceful; Business and Academic Circles Telegraph Request for Punishment; Public Security Bureau Issues Notice to Reassure the People 87

Xiamen Communication: After news of the Xi'an Incident reached Xiamen, the whole city was greatly shaken. Although that day was a Sunday and various circles were on holiday, individuals were running around spreading the news. Whenever people met, they invariably discussed the matter with great tension. This spread to the lower classes of people on the streets. The morning newspapers were sold out. However, the market remained extremely stable. On Monday the 14th, various agencies and organizations held meetings to discuss the matter. In the evening, the Xiamen Chamber of Commerce, various trade associations, the Municipal Education Association, and various schools jointly telegraphed the National Government, requesting that Zhang Xueliang be punished. Because Xiamen is in a special location and has been deeply stimulated by foreign aggression, the support for the suppression of bandits this time is unprecedentedly enthusiastic. However, rice merchants are taking the opportunity to manipulate prices. The price of rice, which had been trending down, rose slightly by one or two jiao on the 14th and 15th. The diplomatic community remains silent. The Quanzhou Xinbao, a Japanese agency, published an inaccurate special edition on the 15th concerning Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. The Public Security Bureau immediately ordered the police to arrest the newsboys along the street and confiscate the newspapers. The Gulangyu Municipal Council took the same action. The Municipal Government also lodged a protest with the Japanese Consul, who warned the newspaper in advance. (December 16)

Wuhu Authorities: Alert to Local Security, Stabilizing Prices; Special Commissioner's Office Announces Informal Martial Law 88

Wuhu Communication: Upon learning of the major change in Xi'an, officials and civilians here were shocked. The price of newspapers from both local and outside cities suddenly increased sharply. Even with maximized printing quantities, supply could not meet demand. The people's concern for national affairs is now vastly different from the past. Thousands of teachers and students from eight middle schools, including Wuhu Middle School and Advanced Agricultural School, gathered at the Wuhu Middle School playground at 3 p.m. on the 14th amidst the bitter wind. First, they stood solemnly for three hours, quietly listening to Huang Anlu, the director of the political training department of the stationed army, and Gao Wenbo, the special commissioner of the Second Administrative District and concurrently the Magistrate of Wuhu County, report on the current situation. Afterwards, they resolved to pass two telegrams in the name of the United Middle Schools, unanimously condemning Zhang Xueliang, urging him to uphold righteousness and escort Chairman Chiang safely back to the capital, and unanimously supporting the Central Government nationwide, using the power of public opinion to urge Zhang to repent. The Wuhu All-Circles Suppression of Bandits, Elimination of Traitors, Resistance to Insults, and National Salvation Conference, which was recently organized, as well as similar organizations in various counties in southern Anhui, also sent telegrams to the Central Government, sincerely supporting Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's return to the capital to preside over the overall situation. The Administrative Commissioner's Office, in view of the people's tense emotions, although superficially calm as usual, feared that villains would take the opportunity to spread rumors, inevitably affecting people's hearts. Moreover, Wuhu is a city where Chinese and foreigners live together, close to the capital. In order to consolidate local security and people's livelihood, it implemented informal martial law on the 15th. After 11 p.m. every night, pedestrians will be inspected. Villains who fabricate rumors will be carefully investigated and apprehended. On the one hand, the industrial and commercial circles were strictly ordered to maintain the normal state of various commodity prices and not to take the opportunity to raise prices and disrupt the market. Also, at 9 a.m. on the morning of the 15th, more than 1,000 representatives from all walks of life in Wuhu were convened at the Xinhua Grand Theater on Zhongshan Road. Commissioner Gao presided over the meeting, announcing the government's handling of the Shaanxi Incident and instructing the people at all levels to maintain their usual attitude of living and working in peace. Subsequently, it was decided that the conference would send telegrams to the Central Government and Zhang Xueliang. The meeting adjourned at noon. (December 15)

Changshu 89

Opening Up the County's Main Road

The streets in the urban area of this county are traditionally very narrow, making transportation inconvenient. Now that the Xihu Railway has opened to traffic, there is a great need to widen the county's main road. The county government is planning to widen the first main line from the South Gate to the North Gate to eight meters to facilitate traffic. This has been approved by the Construction Department. However, according to the opinions of the stationed army, it must be widened to twelve meters to facilitate transportation. It is also proposed to change the route, starting from the South Gate, passing through South Gate Street, South County Street, Daonan Street, County Back Street, North City Center, West Lane, and reaching North Gate Street, close to the northern suburbs, and then widening the northern suburbs to reach the port and connect with the Yangfu Highway, so that it can be bypassed. After consultation, in order to reduce losses, it has been uniformly changed to widening ten meters, and it is scheduled to start work within a few days and be completed within two months. However, the archway of the city gate does not meet the original budget and must be planned separately, delaying the start of construction. After the first line is completed, it will start from the West Gate and open up through Siqian Street, etc., to connect the lines so that it can be looped.

Wujiang 90

Joint Defense Office Executes Traitors

The Joint Defense Office of Taihu Lake Water Police of Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provinces, in the last month, arrested the traitor Zhenjiang Xiao Shizi, namely Li Asi, and the bandit Qin Er in this county. After interrogation, they confessed to plotting wrongdoing and robbing with weapons without denying it. A special request was submitted to the Military Affairs Commission for approval to execute them by shooting. After Director Chen received the order, he identified the two criminals, bound them, and took them to the Mudun outside the East Gate for execution by shooting as a warning to the public.

Establishment of a Tramp Training Institute

The tramp training institute in this county, since Magistrate Xu appointed Wu Xuexin to prepare, has been nearly two months, and preparations have been completed. The opening ceremony is scheduled for the 16th. The institute first has a printing department, a coal base department, and a labor service department. In the future, when funds are sufficient, it will be necessary to increase parts to meet social needs.

Wuxi 91

Judges of the Court Switch Positions

Ren Guanghai, the prosecutor of the local court of this county, has recently received an order from the Judicial Administration Department to go to the Nanjing Judge Training Institute to receive training. After Ren Jun received the order, he set off to Beijing yesterday to receive training. When the term expires, he will return to this county to serve. Also, Liu Bingzhen, a judge of the Criminal Court, was ordered to switch positions with Sheng Shengxiu, a judge of the Nantong Court. Judge Sheng has completed his training and came to Wuxi yesterday to take over and hear cases.

Organizing Labor Service

The labor service for the twenty-fifth year in this county has long been ordered by the county government to the districts for investigation and reporting. However, this service is not limited to dredging rivers, such as repairing dikes, attacking ponds, building roads, and afforestation, as well as self-defense Dingcheng, etc., all of which can be used to organize. The project does not dislike being small or large, and the promotion strives to be universal. Yesterday, Magistrate Long again ordered the district chiefs to formulate separate rules based on local conditions and report them within the year for verification and handling.

Nantong 92

Joint Defense by Military Police in Tong Area

In order to prevent traitors from causing disturbances in the counties of Tong, the water and land police teams have specially resolved to divide the responsible defense areas. In addition, the mountain military police joint inspection office sent a team to take charge of patrolling. In the hinterland areas, the township protection system is implemented by the township and town Baos, and the strongmen patrol system is strictly enforced. The Special Commissioner's Office specially ordered the county magistrates to go to the villages to inspect and urge implementation.

County Government Strictly Pursues Overdue Taxes

The accumulated overdue annual taxes in Tongyi over the years amount to more than one million yuan. The county government specially joined local agencies to form a committee to pursue overdue taxes. Since the business owners have already collected rent, the pressure is on to squeeze and pursue. The number of receipts has been very high in recent days, and 400,000 yuan has been collected.

Taixian 93

Rising Grain Prices Affect Commerce

Since this autumn harvest in Taixian, grain market prices have been rising steadily. In the past few days, the rising trend has been strong. The price of wheat has risen by more than ten yuan, which is unprecedented in recent years. According to the recent Jiangxun market price, pointed rice is 4 yuan and 2 jiao, bald rice is 4 yuan, Zhan rice is 4 yuan and 7 jiao, pointed rice is 10 yuan, bald rice is 9 yuan and 5 jiao, tea rice is 10 yuan and 4 jiao, barley is 4 yuan and 8 jiao 5, wheat is 10 yuan and 8 jiao, new yuan wheat is 6 yuan and 5 jiao. In addition, soybeans, sesame, buckwheat, black beans, etc. have all risen more or less than before. Taixian has always been a food gathering and distribution market for counties in Jiangbei and the lower reaches of the river. Every year, the county's commerce relies on the turnover of trade after the autumn. Recently, due to the rising grain prices, foreign merchants are no longer buying poorly, and many rice customers are turning to Nantong Erjiagang and other places. The land trade in Chen and Jiangquhai districts has been extremely bleak, and general commerce has also declined and languished.

Bengbu 94

Busy Cargo Transportation on the Southern Section of the Jinpu Railway

Due to the busy transportation on the Jinpu Railway recently, there are not enough freight vehicles to allocate, and cargo transportation in various places has been greatly affected. In the southern section between Xu and Pei, there is a particular lack of freight vehicles. As a result, the goods waiting to be transported at various stations are piled up like mountains, with food accounting for the majority. The recent invisible stagnation of the grain market here and the reduction in the transportation of miscellaneous grains are due to this impact. In addition, there is also a lack of coal transportation vehicles, and the number of coal transports has been greatly reduced. The coal from Huainan Datong has also been difficult to transport due to the shallow water of the Huai River, causing the price of coal to look up. The price of firewood and coal in Lieshan has risen by 1 jiao per bushel. Most grain merchants believe that it is difficult to transport by Jinpu Road, so they entrust the goods to the Huaihe Wheel Industry Cooperative to transport them to Tian, and then transfer them to Huainan, Jiangnan, Jinghu, and Shanghai to transport them to Shanghai. In recent days, the goods transported out have been mainly miscellaneous grains such as soybeans and sesame. The Joint Transport Office of the Huaihe Railway Huaihe Joint Transport in Bengbu is responsible for handling the joint transport matters. The Bengbu Chamber of Commerce has telegraphed the Railway Bureau, requesting that vehicles be allocated to dredge the bond transportation within the possible range to help businesses in difficulty.

Ningbo 95

Money Industry Stipulates Settlement Period

The Yin County Money Industry Association held a regular meeting on the 14th and decided that December 31 would be the settlement date for this year, and January 1, 26, 23, and 3 would be closed for two days, but the large-scale closing of accounts with customers would still be handled as usual.

The captain, Mao Zimei, led the police to arrest them. When they arrived, there were indeed nine private traffickers who were carrying them. The tax police immediately opened fire to warn them, and the private traffickers abandoned the salt and fled. A total of two large boats of smuggled salt, weighing more than 40,000 kilograms,

Shaoxing 97

Workers Fight with Weapons in Shizishan

Yesterday in Shizishan, Qianmei Township, Shaoxing, a conflict broke out between the villagers and the railway workers who were buying stone materials. In an instant, hundreds of villagers gathered and fought with each other for two hours. As a result, six people were seriously injured, including Zheng Bingfu, Zhou Songlin, Chen Yinghe, Zhang Liuyi, Wang Zhongcai, and Tong Afu, and more than ten people were slightly injured. The injured have now submitted their injuries to the court for verification and requested the arrest and interrogation of the murderers. The township chief of the area urgently gathered both parties on the 15th to conduct mediation.

Hangzhou 98

Hangyu Section of Hangzhou-Yushan Railway to Change Tracks Next Month

The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway's Hangyu section will be replaced with heavy rails, with a special loan of 2.8 million from the bank and a loan of 6 million from Jie Shang Materials Company for material costs. This has been resolved by the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Board of Directors meeting. Zeng Yangfu will come to Hangzhou from Beijing to preside over the Standing Committee of the Silk Control Association, and will meet with the silver group representative Jin Runquan and others to sign a contract in early January and establish the company. The track replacement project will also begin at the same time and is scheduled to be completed by the end of June.

Shanghai-Shaanxi Communication: Changes in Land and Air Routes Due to Obstructions 102

Since the events in Shaanxi, land and air transportation between Shanghai and Xi'an have been greatly affected. Although wireless communication was briefly restored the night before last, it encountered further obstacles yesterday morning. Other transportation services have also undergone changes. The key information obtained yesterday is summarized as follows:

Wireless Communication Blocked Again Yesterday 103

According to the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Communications last night, wireless communication between Shanghai and Shaanxi, after being restored the night before last, (1) wired communication was disrupted again at 9:25 AM yesterday, making it impossible to communicate with areas beyond Tongguan; (2) wireless communication could not communicate directly after 5:00 PM yesterday and had to be relayed through Hankou.

Longhai Passenger Trains Reach Huayin 104

According to a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency, citing the Shanghai office of the Longhai Railway Water-Land Joint Transportation Office, Longhai Railway passenger trains are operating as usual, reaching Huayin above Tongguan. Freight trains, however, have been temporarily suspended. Shipping Bureau ships such as the Haiyun, Haixian, and Hairui continue to operate regularly on the Shanghai-Lianyungang-Qingdao lines, loading goods from Lianyungang. Because Lianyungang has over 10,000 tons of goods bound for Qingdao, Shanghai, and Guangdong, the transportation of goods from Shanghai and Qingdao to Lianyungang has been temporarily suspended due to transportation issues.

Temporary Measures for the Eurasia Air Route 105

The Eurasia Company's Lanzhou to Baotou route has been temporarily suspended due to reports of unrest in Lanzhou. As for the Shanghai to Lanzhou route, the Shanghai-West flight scheduled for the day before yesterday (Tuesday) was canceled. Tomorrow (Friday)'s Shanghai-West flight is planned to operate as usual to Zhengzhou, while the Zhengzhou to Xi'an and Lanzhou section will be temporarily suspended. As for the Xi'an to Kunming route, it has been decided to reroute flights from Zhengzhou to Luoyang, then to Chengdu, and finally to Kunming. This has reportedly been approved by the Ministry of Communications.

Telegraphic and Air Transfers Suspended Yesterday 106

According to news from the Domestic Exchange Department of the Bank of China yesterday, remittance services to all areas of Shaanxi Province, such as Xi'an, Weinan, Chishui, Lintong, and Sanyuan, have been suspended for telegraphic and air transfers, while mail transfers are still being accepted. According to news from the Domestic Exchange Department of the Bank of Communications, remittance services to all areas of Shaanxi Province above Lintongguan, including telegraphic, air, and mail transfers, have been temporarily suspended due to the chaotic situation in those areas, and because merchants are unwilling to remit funds there.

Parcel Post Still Suspended, Letters Delivered as Usual 107

According to the Shanghai Postal Administration last night, parcel post from Shanghai to all areas of Shaanxi (above Tongguan) remains temporarily suspended. However, letters, including express and registered mail, are still being accepted and delivered as usual. The postal service will make every effort to deliver express mail as quickly as possible within its capabilities. As for air express mail, it will be accepted as usual, as no notice has been received from the Eurasia Aviation Corporation.

Foreigners' Whereabouts During the Shaanxi Incident 108

The Continental News reports that Mr. Powell, a Far East cameraman for the American Fox Film Corporation, departed from Shanghai for Beiping this morning (the 16th). If possible, he will go to Xi'an to film the major events in China. His assistant, Mr. Vargassoff, who is currently in Beiping, will also accompany him. Mr. Vargassoff is also currently serving as Zhang Xueliang's personal photographer. According to Mr. Powell last night, although he is also a friend of Mr. Zhang, the resistance to going to Xi'an is quite strong, and he fears he may not be able to achieve his objective. It was also reported yesterday that Mr. Huang, a news photographer for the American Hearst Metrotone News, has already gone to Xi'an from Qingdao. Mr. King, a reporter for the New York Times News Agency, is also reportedly departing from Beiping, intending to reach Xi'an. Mr. Smasseth, a reporter for the Chicago Daily News, is also trying to go. It is noted that the publisher of the Chicago Daily News is Mr. Knox, the Republican vice-presidential candidate who lost in the recent US presidential election.

The Continental News reports that Mr. Lutz, the pilot of the Eurasia Aviation Corporation, and Mr. Fischer, the co-pilot, were initially of concern for their safety. However, yesterday morning (the 15th), the company received news from Mr. Lutz from Lanzhou stating that the two were being detained there and would be able to fly the Junkers large aircraft to Shanghai as soon as the situation stabilized. The company also received news from another aircraft from Ningxia stating that Mr. Menchiel, the pilot, and Mr. Stechnozi, the co-pilot, flew to Zhengzhou at noon. Before the aircraft returns to Shanghai, it will make several special flights for the Zhengzhou authorities. To maintain transportation, the Eurasia Aviation Corporation plans to send an aircraft on Friday via Nanjing and Chengdu to Yunnan. Unless the situation in Xi'an improves significantly, it will not stop in that city as usual for the time being. According to Eurasia Aviation Corporation officials, the rapid restoration of order in Xi'an is crucial from the standpoint of China's commercial aviation. Thousands of people directly or indirectly rely on Eurasia's aircraft. Xi'an has become a hub for Northwest aviation operated by the Sino-German company and a very important aviation station.

Contract for Chengdu-Chongqing Railway Loan Signed Yesterday: Total of 34.5 Million, Loan Provided by French Banking Group, Signed by Representative of China Construction Bank 113

Yesterday, the Sichuan-Guizhou Railway Company, for the purpose of constructing the Chengdu-Chongqing Railway, signed a contract for a loan of 34.5 million yuan with the French banking group, represented by the China Construction Bank and the Banque Franco-Chinoise. Song Ziwen, Executive Director of the China Construction Bank, issued the following statement regarding the loan:

Today, the China Construction Bank, representing the Sichuan-Guizhou Railway Company, signed a loan contract with the Banque Franco-Chinoise, representing the French banking group, for the construction of the railway between Chengdu and Chongqing. The railway is 523 kilometers long and passes through a prosperous area in central Sichuan. It is expected to be completed within two and a half years. The construction cost is estimated at 54.5 million yuan, of which 20 million yuan will be borne by the Sichuan-Guizhou Railway Company, and 34.5 million yuan will be borrowed from the French banking group. Of this amount, 27.5 million yuan is for the cost of materials and freight to Chongqing, and the remaining 7 million yuan is for cash. The loan will be repaid in 15 years and is unconditionally guaranteed by the Ministry of Railways. The Sichuan-Guizhou Railway Company received a business license from the Executive Yuan on March 21 of this year and was formally established today. Its capital is 20 million yuan, of which 11 million yuan is commercial stock underwritten by the China Construction Bank, 4.5 million yuan is allocated by the Ministry of Railways, and the remaining 4.5 million yuan is allocated by the Sichuan Provincial Government. This loan for the construction of the Chengdu-Chongqing Railway is very different from previous railway loans: (1) The railway is a private railway, and its business management is entirely in accordance with commercial companies. If necessary, the government will still provide full assistance, and the government's shares can also be sold to ordinary merchants and people under market conditions. (2) It is a new initiative in recent years for foreigners to provide long-term credit in cash and materials for China's railway construction. (3) The construction, operation, management, and procurement of materials for the railway are all managed by Chinese personnel. The loan contract stipulates that two French personnel will be hired as technical staff. (4) The China Construction Bank is the sole trustee of the French banking group.

South Seas Commercial Inspection Group Hopes to Expand South Seas Routes, Requests China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to Organize 114

Mr. Gao Shiheng, the former leader of the South Seas Commercial Inspection Group, recognizing the importance of the South Seas routes, not only for the convenience of cargo transportation but also for preventing national economic leakage, has repeatedly made suggestions to the government and various parties. Yesterday, he wrote to Director Cai of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, stating the eagerness of domestic and foreign industries and businesses for the South Seas routes, hoping that the company could open the Shanghai to Singapore and Shanghai to Siam routes as soon as possible, or organize joint operations with overseas Chinese shipping companies along the way. The original letter stated: "The patriotic enthusiasm of overseas Chinese in the South Seas is beyond description. They are particularly concerned about the rise and fall of the motherland's shipping industry. They are all pleased with the thriving state of your company and hope that your company can take a further step to open up the South Seas routes, prevent national economic leakage, and facilitate the transportation of national goods. Based on my humble opinion, I would like to request your company to open up the two most essential routes first. The first route is from Shanghai via Xiamen and Hong Kong to Singapore. The second route is from Shanghai via Shantou and Hong Kong to Siam. Each route should have two round trips per month, with cargo transportation as the main business for the time being. The industrial and commercial sectors in Singapore and Siam are dominated by overseas Chinese, so the cargo transportation on both routes will definitely be prosperous. However, in the initial stage of establishment, there may be losses in terms of the company's own income. However, from the perspective of the national economy, every penny earned from the South Seas routes is a leakage that is recovered, and its benefit to the national economy is immeasurable. As a state-owned shipping company, your company should focus on this long-term management and will surely be happy to engage in it. If it is temporarily difficult to open up the above-mentioned routes, then I would like to request that you organize joint operations with overseas Chinese shipping companies. The first route can be contacted with the shipping company run by overseas Chinese in Singapore. The second route can be contacted with the Chen Hongli Shipping Company in Bangkok. The company's ships regularly travel between Siam, Shantou, and Hong Kong, with several trips every ten days. The company is represented by Qian Tailong at 27 Man Wai Street, Hong Kong, and by Bo Ning Company in Shantou. Joint transportation and transshipment in Shantou or Hong Kong are extremely simple and convenient." It is reported that Director Cai Zengji has attached great importance to the points mentioned and has ordered the relevant departments to study them and will send personnel to investigate to make them a reality.

Pang Jingzhou Returns from the Front Lines, Talks in Detail About Opinions on Rescuing the Suiyuan War 116

Mr. Pang Jingzhou of the China Red Cross Society Relief Committee has repeatedly traveled back and forth to handle relief matters since the outbreak of the Suiyuan War. The North China Temporary Branch of the China Red Cross Society Relief Committee has been established to actively implement the work. He has now returned to Shanghai this morning to raise medical supplies. According to Mr. Pang's statement to the Central News Agency reporter, his observations are as follows: "I first stayed in Beiping, then went to Suiyuan, and returned through Zhuozishan, Jining, and Datong, where I conducted on-the-ground inspections and planned relief equipment. I also had in-depth discussions with officers at all levels, so I have a more detailed understanding of the situation. I now offer the following opinions to those who are enthusiastic about comforting and assisting in relief work: (1) Regarding materials, provide large quantities so that they can be universally distributed. Otherwise, the supply will be insufficient and will inevitably be put aside, and the quality should be practical rather than exquisite. (A) Food should only be filling and does not need to be delicate. Biscuits, for example, do not seem to suit the stomach very well. (B) Gloves made of wool thread are not very durable and are best made of leather. (C) Gas masks are currently being developed by Gu Yuzhen, Dean of the College of Engineering of Tsinghua University, and the reporter (D) Silk cotton vests should be replaced with silk cotton clothing, and if they can be made of thick leather, they must be large in size to be warm and useful. (E) Bedding is not needed on the front lines, and there seems to be no need for it in the rear because there are many stoves. (2) Regarding relief workers, (A) Medicines should not be disorganized and should be the main medicines prescribed by the Military Medical Department. (B) Stretchers are not easily available on the front lines, and I hope that all sectors of society will donate them. The Red Cross Society has several samples of different materials on display for donors to refer to. (C) Relief personnel cannot serve on the front lines unless they have been trained and must be militarized. (D) There are very few suitable places for hospitals in Jin and Sui. Outside Datong City, near the Yungang Grottoes (scenic area), there are 300 houses for civilians that were previously donated by Chairman Chiang and others, but they have not yet been occupied. Each room is one zhang wide and one zhang two deep and can be used as a hospital for the wounded, but because there is a earthen pit in each room, which occupies half of the entire room, the entire building can accommodate a maximum of 1,200 wounded soldiers, and it is difficult to arrange hospital beds." In summary, these are the most important points that can be used as a reference for all sectors of society. Although the country has recently undergone major changes, everyone should remain calm and not forget to provide relief for the Suiyuan War. As the war is now advancing into Shangdu, the military situation will inevitably expand, and relief efforts should be stepped up and carried out."

Various Sectors Donate Materials to Comfort Suiyuan Soldiers 117

Mr. Zhu Shien, a citizen, recognizing the rampancy of the Mongolian puppets and the bravery of our soldiers fighting the enemy on the front lines, enduring hunger and cold, donated 1,000 silk cotton cold-weather garments and 1,000 military-use thermos bottles, with 500 spare inner bottles, packed in twelve boxes, and requested the municipal government to arrange for their transportation to the front lines. After receiving the donations, the municipal government has already transported them to Suiyuan Province. In addition, all faculty and students of the Huayang Vocational English Night School donated 42.048 yuan in donations for Suiyuan, which has been transferred to the front lines by the One-Day Income Promotion Committee.

New Timetable of Two Railways to be Implemented on New Year's Day; Capital Express to Run Once Daily in Each Direction; Shortened Travel Time Between Beijing and Zhabei, No Longer via North Station 118

The Joint Administration Bureau of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, upon order from the Ministry [of Railways], will launch a Capital Express train once daily in each direction on the Beijing-Shanghai Line. On the Shanghai-Zhabei section of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Line, one express train will be reduced daily in each direction to align with current engine power conditions. The Traffic Department has already revised the timetables for the Beijing-Shanghai, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo, and Suzhou-Jiaxing sections, which are approved to be implemented on New Year's Day. All staff and employees have been instructed to comply. Details are as follows:

Notice to Staff and Employees

The Traffic Department hereby notifies all staff and employees that, upon order, the Beijing-Shanghai Line will increase the Capital Express by one train daily in each direction, and the Shanghai-Zhabei section of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Line will reduce one express train daily in each direction, to align with the current engine power conditions. It is necessary to revise the timetables for each line accordingly. The speed of the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway has been increased compared to before. All through-trains for passenger connecting service between Beijing and Zhabei will be rerouted via the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway, with transfers at Wuxian and Jiaxing stations respectively, no longer passing through the North Station, in order to shorten travel time. Furthermore, after the timetables of the two railways are changed, the timetables of all trains on the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway should also be revised to ensure connection with the trains on the two railways. The timetables for the two railways and the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway have been revised and are ready to be implemented starting from January 1, 1937. All previous timetable charts issued by this department for the two railways and the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway will be canceled from the same date. The composition of passenger trains, the operation of vehicles on the two railways and the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway, and the train numbering method stipulated in Announcement Yun Zi No. 1210 of June 22, 1934, have also been revised as per the attached tables, effective from the same date. As for the current timetables, operating procedures, and train compositions of the trains on the Songhu and Caoyong sections, as well as the Shanghai-Xiangpu commuter trains, all will remain as before, except for the train numbers on the Caoyong section. The points that should be noted in this revised timetable are listed separately below, along with the No. 8 timetable for railway staff of the two railways and the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway, the train numbering table, the passenger train composition table, and the vehicle operation table, which are hereby distributed for your compliance.

Points to Note

Points to Note for the No. 8 Timetable: A. Regarding the Two Railways and the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway: (1) Section Chiefs of each Traffic Section, Station Masters of each station, and all ticket inspectors should pay close attention to passenger density at all times, notify the Dispatching Section of the Transportation Department, and fill in the ticket inspector's service report, in order to increase or decrease the number of cars attached to the trains. If stations need to increase or decrease the number of cars due to circumstances, they must obtain the prior consent of the Dispatching Section of the Transportation Department. (2) Through-cars for passengers between Beijing and Zhabei will each use one first, second, and third-class baggage car. Down trains are attached to the third train of the Beijing-Shanghai Line to Wuxian Station, transferred to the 255th train of the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway to Jiaxing Station, and transferred to the 31st train of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Line to Zhabei. Up trains are attached to the 12th train of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Line to Jiaxing Station, transferred to the 254th train of the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway to Wuxian Station, and transferred to the 22nd train of the Beijing-Shanghai Line to Beijing. When the through-cars are attached to the trains of the two railways, they should be attached behind the conductor's car at the end. When operating on the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway, they should be attached after the conductor's car at the end.

Beijing-Shanghai Line

B. Regarding the Beijing-Shanghai Line: (3) If passengers at Nanjing and Kunshan stations who have purchased through tickets to ride the 302nd Shanghai-Pinghu through-train declare at their respective stations 20 minutes before the train departs from the North Station, the station masters of each station should telegraph the station master of the North Station to make arrangements in advance. The station master of the North Station will issue a stop order, temporarily stopping the train at the relevant stations. (4) If through passengers on the 301st Shanghai-Pinghu through-train wish to disembark at Kunshan Station or Nanxiang Station, they should declare to the Nanjing Station Master in advance, or when Nanjing Station has received a telegram notification from the Railway, the Nanjing Station Master should issue a stop order, temporarily stopping the train at the relevant stations. (5) When the 44th Shanghai-Zhenjiang second and fourth-class commuter train departs from the North Station, it is not allowed to sell fourth-class tickets from the North Station to the three stations before it: Kunshan, Wuxian, and Wuxi, in order to alleviate congestion. (6) The 4th Shanghai-Beijing Express stops at Shitangwan Station, the 5th Beijing-Shanghai Express and the 7th Beijing-Shanghai Night Express stop at Henglin Station, the 6th Shanghai-Beijing Special Express and the 8th Shanghai-Beijing Night Express stop at Benniu Station, and the 21st Beijing-Shanghai Express stops at Xiashu and Zhoujingxiang Stations. All stops are due to meeting arrangements and no passenger tickets to or from these stations will be sold. If the meeting location changes, or the train to be met has already arrived at the station, the above trains will immediately cancel their stops at the respective stations. (7) The 4th Shanghai-Beijing Special Express and the 5th Beijing-Shanghai Special Express each attach through-cars for Shanghai-Wuhu connection, including one first and second-class car and one third-class baggage, postal, and conductor car, which are transferred at Yaohuamen Station, directly connecting Shanghai and Wuhu. These through-cars are attached at the rear of the train. (8) The 501st and 502nd freight trains are specifically for transporting less-than-carload (LCL) freight. The number of cars is limited to 1,000 metric tons, or the total length of the train is limited to 300 meters. If the LCL freight is not enough for a full train, the Dispatching Office of the Transportation Department may allocate other vehicles as appropriate. Stations along the way that wish to add or detach vehicles must first consult with the Transportation Department and obtain consent before proceeding. If there is no loading or unloading of goods at the designated stopping stations, the stop should be canceled. If unloading is required at stations not designated to stop, a temporary stop may be made. The stop order should be issued by the loading station. If goods are to be loaded, the loading station may also contact the nearest large station in advance and issue a stop order to temporarily stop. However, the Transportation Department must be notified by dispatcher telephone in advance in all cases. All loading and unloading procedures must be completed in the shortest possible time, and strict adherence to on-time arrival at the terminating station must be maintained. 9. If there are not enough goods to fill a train for the 401st, 402nd, 403rd, and 404th connecting freight trains, other freight cars from this railway may be attached.

Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Line

C. Regarding the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Line, 10. The 11th, 12th, 13th, and 14th Shanghai-Zhabei special express trains all detach a portion of the cars to go directly to and depart from Shangnan Station. 11. If staff from the Jianqiao Central Aviation School wish to take the 13th Shanghai-Zhabei special express train from the North Station to Jianqiao Station, they may request the Station Master of the North Station with written proof from the school in advance. Or, if they wish to take the 14th Zhabei-Shanghai special express train from Jianqiao Station to the North Station, they may request the Station Master of the Jianqiao Station with a written request from the school two hours before the train arrives at Jianqiao Station. In either case, the train will be allowed to stop at Jianqiao Station. 12. The 801st and 802nd freight trains are specifically for carrying less-than-carload (LCL) freight. If there is excess engine power, full carload vehicles may be added.

Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway

D. Regarding the Suzhou-Jiaxing Railway, 13. When empty or loaded freight cars are attached to mixed trains, up trains are limited to being attached behind the locomotive, and down trains are limited to being attached before the conductor's car at the rear, in order to suit the existing platform conditions at Wuxian and Jiaxing stations. If livestock cars are attached, the circumstances should be considered to ensure that they are separated from passenger cars by a reasonable distance.
